	/* Event */
.btDarkSkin .bt_bb_event,
.btLightSkin .btDarkSkin .bt_bb_event,

    color: #fff;
    }

    -webkit-flex: 1 0 100%;
    -ms-flex: 1 0 100%;
    flex: 1 0 100%;
    }
.bt_bb_event .bt_bb_event_image:after {
    content: " ";
    display: table;
    width: 100%;
    clear: both;
    line-height: 0;
    }
.bt_bb_event .bt_bb_event_image .bt_bb_image {
    width: 100%;
    }
.bt_bb_event .bt_bb_event_image .bt_bb_image img {
    width: 100%;
    }

    border-top-left-radius: 50px;
    border-top-right-radius: 50px;
    overflow: hidden;
    }

    border-top-left-radius: 10px;
    border-top-right-radius: 10px;
    overflow: hidden;

<h1 class="gb-headline gb-headline-1f9fb7c1 gb-headline-text">After School Care Services in Singapore</h1>
<h4 class="wp-block-heading" id="from-the-creators-of-the-no-1-preschooland-enrichment-academy"><strong>From the Creators of the No.1 Preschool and Enrichment Academy </strong></h4>
<p> <mark style="background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)" class="has-inline-color has-base-3-color">MindSpace is the only after school care centre in Singapore that incorporates the proprietary</mark>.<mark style="background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)" class="has-inline-color has-base-3-color"> MindChamps research evidence-based pedagogy. </mark><br><mark style="background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)" class="has-inline-color has-base-3-color">Here at MindSpace, we enable your child to develop the Champion Mindset.</mark> </p>

<div class="gb-grid-column gb-grid-column-4ff7e65b"><div class="gb-container gb-container-4ff7e65b"><div class="gb-inside-container">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="break-the-cycle-of-endless-tuition"><strong><mark style="background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)" class="has-inline-color has-global-color-9-color">Break the Cycle of Endless Tuition</mark></strong></h2>
<p>Traditional rote learning methods are no longer effective in helping children cope with the academic pressure in Singapore. MindSpace provides student care services and weekend enrichment that will equip your child with a proven method of learning that eliminates the need for tuition and helps your child understand everything they learn in school.</p>
</div></div></div>
</div>
<div class="gb-grid-wrapper gb-grid-wrapper-53fe1040">
<div class="gb-grid-column gb-grid-column-e7298104"><div class="gb-container gb-container-e7298104"><div class="gb-inside-container">
<h1 class="wp-block-heading" id="insanity-is-doing-the-same-thing-over-and-over-and-expecting-different-results"><mark style="background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)" class="has-inline-color has-global-color-8-color">“Insanity is doing</mark> <strong><mark style="background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)" class="has-inline-color has-global-color-8-color">the same thing over </mark></strong> <strong><mark style="background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)" class="has-inline-color has-global-color-8-color">and over and expecting different results.”</mark></strong></h1>
<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong><em>– Albert Einstein</em></strong></p>
</div></div></div>
<div class="gb-grid-column gb-grid-column-8fade497"><div class="gb-container gb-container-8fade497"><div class="gb-inside-container">
<div class="wp-block-image is-style-default">

<div class="gb-grid-column gb-grid-column-f34568f1"><div class="gb-container gb-container-f34568f1"><div class="gb-inside-container">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="integrating-our-proven-research-backed-curriculum"><strong><mark style="background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)" class="has-inline-color has-global-color-9-color">Integrating Our Proven Research-Backed Curriculum</mark></strong></h2>
<p>More than just care and supervision, the after school care services by MindSpace incorporates our renowned&nbsp;<a href="https://mindspace.mindchamps.org/curriculum/">MindChamps enrichment curriculum</a>&nbsp;that complements the MOE syllabus. Instead of repetition and memorisation, our student care and weekend enrichment reinforces subject-specific knowledge and develops our students’ understanding of new concepts through the Optimal Flow Method™.</p>
</div></div></div>
</div>
</div></div>
<div class="gb-container gb-container-734944f1 bg-gradient"><div class="gb-inside-container">

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-base-3-color has-text-color" id="why-choose-mindspace">Why Choose MindSpace?</h2>
<div style="height:15px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>
<div class="gb-grid-wrapper gb-grid-wrapper-b8123ec1">
<div class="gb-grid-column gb-grid-column-1e12963e"><div class="gb-container gb-container-1e12963e"><div class="gb-inside-container">

<div style="height:30px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-base-3-color has-text-color" id="the-champion-mindset">The Champion Mindset</h3>
<p></p>
<p class="has-text-align-center has-base-3-color has-text-color">Our after school student care empowers your child with the skills, abilities, and most importantly, the Champion Mindset to thrive in an unpredictable future</p>
</div></div></div>

<div style="height:30px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-base-3-color has-text-color" id="the-art-of-learning">The Art of Learning</h3>
<p></p>
<p class="has-text-align-center has-base-3-color has-text-color">Your child will be taught how to learn through proprietary learning techniques that complement the concepts taught in school.</p>
</div></div></div>
<div class="gb-grid-column gb-grid-column-ffb05483"><div class="gb-container gb-container-ffb05483"><div class="gb-inside-container">
<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="148" height="176" src="https://mindspace.mindchamps.org/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/the-optimalflow-method.png" alt="" class="wp-image-2446" style="width:74px;height:88px"></figure></div>
<div style="height:30px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-base-3-color has-text-color" id="the-optimal-flow-method">The Optimal Flow Method</h3>
<p></p>
<p class="has-text-align-center has-base-3-color has-text-color">Your child will learn the necessary techniques and skills to help them achieve breakthroughs in their academic journey.</p>
</div></div></div>
</div>

<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-base-3-color has-text-color" id="nutritious-meals">Nutritious Meals</h3>
<p></p>
<p class="has-text-align-center has-base-3-color has-text-color">Your child will enjoy varied, deliciously prepared meals together with supplements that provide all the nourishment that they need to grow up strong and healthy, both physically and mentally.</p>

<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-base-3-color has-text-color" id="family-time-and-bonding">Family Time and Bonding</h3>
<p></p>
<p class="has-text-align-center has-base-3-color has-text-color">Your time with your child is precious. MindSpace takes away the need for tuition with our curated after school care programmes, so that you can spend more time connecting with your child.</p>

<p></p>
<p class="has-text-align-center has-base-3-color has-text-color">Our after school student care centres have developed rigorous training programmes for our Specialist Subject Coaches so that they are best equipped not only to teach but also motivate and inspire through their passion and dedication.</p>

<section id="section-9df8ae74-7c29-4d89-b3fc-2ada5b824509" class="wp-block-gutentor-accordion gutentor-section gutentor-accordion-wrapper accordion-template1"><div class="grid-container"><div class="gutentor-block-header"><div class="gutentor-section-title text-center"><h2 class="gutentor-title">Frequently Asked Questions <br>About After School Care</h2></div></div><div class="grid-row gutentor-grid-item-wrap"><div class="grid-md-12"><div class="gutentor-accordion-wrap"><div class="gutentor-single-item gutentor-single-item-0"><div class="gutentor-single-item-wrap"><div class="gutentor-accordion-heading"><i class="gutentor-accordion-icon open-icon fas fa-plus"></i><i class="gutentor-accordion-icon close-icon fas fa-minus"></i><h3 class="gutentor-single-item-title"><strong>1. Which is the nearest MindSpace after school care centre near me?</strong></h3></div><div class="gutentor-accordion-body"><p class="gutentor-single-item-desc">We have multiple MindSpace after school care centres across Singapore, each and every one specifically designed to facilitate the ultimate after school learning environment—think clean spacious classrooms, state-of-the-art interactive screens, and dedicated areas for meals and social interactions.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="gutentor-accordion-wrap"><div class="gutentor-single-item gutentor-single-item-1"><div class="gutentor-single-item-wrap"><div class="gutentor-accordion-heading"><i class="gutentor-accordion-icon open-icon fas fa-plus"></i><i class="gutentor-accordion-icon close-icon fas fa-minus"></i><h3 class="gutentor-single-item-title"><strong>2. How much are MindSpace student care centre fees in Singapore?</strong></h3></div><div class="gutentor-accordion-body"><p class="gutentor-single-item-desc"><a href="https://mindspace.mindchamps.org/contact-us/">Reach out to us </a>to find out more about our student care programmes and fees.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="gutentor-accordion-wrap"><div class="gutentor-single-item gutentor-single-item-2"><div class="gutentor-single-item-wrap"><div class="gutentor-accordion-heading"><i class="gutentor-accordion-icon open-icon fas fa-plus"></i><i class="gutentor-accordion-icon close-icon fas fa-minus"></i><h3 class="gutentor-single-item-title"><strong>3. What ages of children are eligible for MindSpace student care in Singapore?</strong></h3></div><div class="gutentor-accordion-body"><p class="gutentor-single-item-desc">MindSpace offers after school care programmes for primary school students from P1 to P5, from 1.00 pm to 7.00pm. Check out our curated <a href="https://mindspace.mindchamps.org/mindchamp-primary-success-for-https:/mindspace.mindchamps.org/mindchamp-primary-success-for-primary-1-2/primary-1-2/">curriculum for P1 – P2 students</a>, or learn more about our after school care <a href="https://mindspace.mindchamps.org/mindchamp-primary-success-for-primary-3-5/">programme for P3 – P5 students</a>.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></section>

<script type="text/javascript">
			function showhide_toggle(type, post_id, more_text, less_text) {
				var   $link = jQuery("#"+ type + "-link-" + post_id)
					, $link_a = jQuery('a', $link)
					, $content = jQuery("#"+ type + "-content-" + post_id)
					, $toggle = jQuery("#"+ type + "-toggle-" + post_id)
					, show_hide_class = 'sh-show sh-hide';
				$link.toggleClass(show_hide_class);
				$content.toggleClass(show_hide_class).toggle();
				if($link_a.attr('aria-expanded') === 'true') {
					$link_a.attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
				} else {
					$link_a.attr('aria-expanded', 'true');
				}
				if($toggle.text() === more_text) {
					$toggle.text(less_text);
					$link.trigger( "sh-link:more" );
				} else {
					$toggle.text(more_text);
					$link.trigger( "sh-link:less" );
				}
				$link.trigger( "sh-link:toggle" );
			}
